      <div class="loadmore"> 
       <div id="show" class="showmore">
        <a class="a" style="display: block;line-height: 49px;" href="javascript:;">More</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <script>
jQuery(function(){
	var url=window.location.href.split("#");
	var href=url[0];
	var hash=url[1];
	if (hash===undefined || hash=="" || !hash){
		var n=1;
	}
	else{
		var n=parseInt(hash);
	}
	
	//计算滚动条高度
	if (n>1){
		var top=600+416*3*(n-1);
		jQuery('html,body').animate({scrollTop:top},1000);
	}
	
    giveMore("#show","#box",12*n,12,500);
});

    function giveMore(button,targetUl,showNumber,loadNumber,speed){
        var list = showNumber;
        var ul = jQuery(targetUl);
        var sum = ul.find("li").hide().length;
        if(sum > list) jQuery(button).css("visibility","visible");
        ul.find("li:lt(" + list + ")").show();
        jQuery(button).on("click",function(){
            list += loadNumber;
            ul.find("li:lt(" + list + ")").slideDown(speed?speed:400);
            if(list >= sum) jQuery(this).css("visibility","hidden");
			
			//重构 url
			var url=window.location.href.split("#");
			var href=url[0];
			var hash=parseInt(url[1]);
			if (hash===undefined || hash=="" || !hash){
				var hash=1;
			}
			href+="#"+String(hash+1);
			history.pushState(null,null,href);
        });
    }

    $.each($(".list-main"), function() {
        if($(this).find("li").length<10){
            $(".loadmore").addClass("zs_hide");
        }
    });

</script> <!--尾部-->
